	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php');
	writefile_35();
	if (!is_file('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php') != '44285f92e72b9ca65ff2d037ee5ad723d5760d05') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php') !== '44285f92e72b9ca65ff2d037ee5ad723d5760d05') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php') !== '2cee4b30bf05faf97523815f38e68a773394c9d7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_35();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php') !== '44285f92e72b9ca65ff2d037ee5ad723d5760d05') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabasePluginSQLite3.class.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_36();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'de66b8dd4d8349dbdaf6c39789f9eda77e040c62') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'de66b8dd4d8349dbdaf6c39789f9eda77e040c62') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'f1ecfd63806fc71929e2b6981f031fe2b485220e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_36();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'de66b8dd4d8349dbdaf6c39789f9eda77e040c62') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/index.php');
	writefile_49();
	if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/index.php') != '86ee51ef61bd29d0018997a13fe05828114d30d6') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '86ee51ef61bd29d0018997a13fe05828114d30d6') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== 'c4d64150cb653186886cbe2600fba879f87225e1') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_49();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '86ee51ef61bd29d0018997a13fe05828114d30d6') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
		}
	}
}
